<p>HMS (<strong>H</strong>ealth <strong>M</strong>anagement <strong>S</strong>ystem) is a function set up to facilitate
    the users of the Bambu Lab printer and AMS to troubleshoot the issues. The users can take advantage of notifications
    from HMS to know the system's status, including some mechanical and hardware errors, or the reason for printing
    failures. We've set up a wiki page with a detailed description and troubleshooting for each error code. Therefore,
    when you see the message prompted by HMS, you can scan the QR code with your mobile phone to go to the corresponding
    page to check the cause of the fault and the troubleshooting steps.</p>
<ul>
    <li><a href="https://wiki.bambulab.com/x1/troubleshooting/intro-hms">HMS Introduction</a></li>
    <li><a href="https://wiki.bambulab.com/en/x1/troubleshooting/how-to-enter-the-specific-code-page">How to enter the
            HMS code page on your printer</a></li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
    <p><i><strong>HMS Search Tips</strong></i></p>
    <p>1. You can search in the search box at the top.</p>
    <p>2. Search HMS code with every 4 characters separated by a dash: <mark
            class="pen-red"><strong>0300-0C00-0001-0004.</strong></mark></p>
<p>3.Use the search function of your PC browser (e.g., the shortcut key Ctrl+F) to search the current HMS page, and enter an HMS code in the specified format: <strong>0300-0C00-0001-0004</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p style="text-align:center;"><span class="text-huge"><strong>HMS Code Index</strong></span></p>
<h2>Machine controller</h2>
<blockquote>
    <p><strong>HMS_0300-2700-0001-0008: The nozzle offset calibration sensor signal is too weak. It may be that the nozzle is sticky or the nozzle does not move above the sensor during calibration, causing the distance between the nozzle and the sensor to be too far.</strong></p>
    <p><strong>Synonyms: </strong>0300-2700-0001-0008</p>
    <ul>
        <li><a href="https://wiki.bambulab.com/en/h2d/troubleshooting/hmscode/0300_2700_0001_0008" class="is-internal-link is-valid-page">H2D/H2D Pro/H2C</a></li>
    </ul>
</blockquote>


<blockquote>
    <p><strong>HMS_1A00-E000-0001-0005: The Induction Hotend Rack is blocked by an obstacle during homing. Please clear any obstructions from its movement path.</strong></p>

<h2>Micro Lidar &amp; AI</h2>

<blockquote>
    <p><strong>HMS_0C00-0300-0002-0015：Foreign object detection is not working. Detected the Live View Camera has been replaced. Please tap "Settings>Calibration" on printer screen and re-calibrate the Live View Camera.</strong></p>
    <p><strong>Synonyms:</strong> 0C00-0300-0002-0015</p>
    <ul>
        <li><a href="/en/p2s/troubleshooting/hmscode/0C00_0300_0002_0015" class="is-internal-link is-valid-page">P2S</a></li>
    </ul>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
    <p><strong>HMS_0500-0600-0002-0034：Live View camera is not connected. Please check the hardware and cable connections.</strong></p>
    <p><strong>Synonyms:</strong> 0500-0600-0002-0034</p>
    <ul>
        <li><a href="/en/p2s/troubleshooting/hmscode/0500_0600_0002_0034" class="is-internal-link is-valid-page">P2S</a></li>
    </ul>

    <p><span class="text-small"><strong>Synonyms:</strong> </span><span class="text-tiny">07FE-4500-0002-0002,
            07FF-4500-0002-0002, 18FE-4500-0002-0002, 18FF-4500-0002-0002</span></p>
    <ul>
        <li><a href="https://wiki.bambulab.com/en/h2/troubleshooting/hmscode/07FE_4500_0002_0002">H2 series</a></li>
    </ul>
</blockquote>

            issue. Please include a picture or video illustrating the problem, as well as any additional information
            related to your inquiry.</i></p>
